If not see\n<http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.  */\n\n/* warning, error, and fatal.  These definitions are suitable for use\n   in the generator programs; the compiler has a more elaborate suite\n   of diagnostic printers, found in diagnostic-global-context.cc using\n   the diagnostics/ subdirectory.  */\n\n#ifdef HOST_GENERATOR_FILE\n#include \"config.h\"\n#define GENERATOR_FILE 1\n#else\n#include \"bconfig.h\"\n#endif\n#include \"system.h\"\n#include \"errors.h\"\n\n/* Set this to argv[0] at the beginning of main.  */\n\nconst char *progname;\n\n/* Starts out 0, set to 1 if error is called.  */\n\nint have_error = 0;\n\n/* Print a warning message - output produced, but there may be problems.  */\n\nvoid\nwarning (const char *format, ...)\n{\n  va_list ap;\n\n  va_start (ap, format);\n  fprintf (stderr, \"%s: warning: \", progname);\n  vfprintf (stderr, format, ap);\n  va_end (ap);\n  fputc ('\\n', stderr);\n}\n\n\n/* Print an error message - we keep going but the output is unusable.  */\n\nvoid\nerror (const char *format, ...)\n{\n  va_list ap;\n\n  va_start (ap, format);\n  fprintf (stderr, \"%s: \", progname);\n  vfprintf (stderr, format, ap);\n  va_end (ap);\n  fputc ('\\n', stderr);\n\n  have_error = 1;\n}\n\n\n/* Fatal error - terminate execution immediately.  Does not return.  */\n\nvoid\nfatal (const char *format, ...)\n{\n  va_list ap;\n\n  va_start (ap, format);\n  fprintf (stderr, \"%s: \", progname);\n  vfprintf (stderr, format, ap);\n  va_end (ap);\n  fputc ('\\n', stderr);\n  exit (FATAL_EXIT_CODE);\n}\n\n/* Similar, but say we got an internal error.  */\n\nvoid\ninternal_error (const char *format, ...)\n{\n  va_list ap;\n\n  va_start (ap, format);\n  fprintf (stderr, \"%s: Internal error: \", progname);\n  vfprintf (stderr, format, ap);\n  va_end (ap);\n  fputc ('\\n', stderr);\n  exit (FATAL_EXIT_CODE);\n}\n\n/* Given a partial pathname as input, return another pathname that\n   shares no directory elements with the pathname of __FILE__.  This\n   is used by fancy_abort() to print `Internal compiler error in expr.cc'\n   instead of `Internal compiler error in ../../GCC/gcc/expr.cc'.  This\n   version is meant to be used for the gen* programs and therefor need not\n   handle subdirectories.  */\n\nconst char *\ntrim_filename (const char *name)\n{\n  static const char this_file[] = __FILE__;\n  const char *p = name, *q = this_file;\n\n  /* Skip any parts the two filenames have in common.  */\n  while (*p == *q && *p != 0 && *q != 0)\n    p++, q++;\n\n  /* Now go backwards until the previous directory separator.  */\n  while (p > name && !IS_DIR_SEPARATOR (p[-1]))\n    p--;\n\n  return p;\n}\n\n/* \"Fancy\" abort.  Reports where in the compiler someone gave up.\n   This file is used only by build programs, so we're not as polite as\n   the version in diagnostics/context.cc.  */\nvoid\nfancy_abort (const char *file, int line, const char *func)\n{\n  internal_error (\"abort in %s, at %s:%d\", func, trim_filename (file), line);\n}\n","numLines":136,"startLine":1,"totalLines":136}}}

Use rarely.\n   It is ignored for machine-readable output formats.  */\nvoid\nverbatim (const char *gmsgid, ...)\n{\n  auto logger = global_dc->get_logger ();\n  log_function_params (logger, ret;\n}\n\n/* As above, but for rich_location *.  */\n\nbool\nemit_diagnostic (enum diagnostics::kind kind,\n\t\t rich_location *richloc,\n\t\t diagnostics::option_id option_id,\n\t\t const char option_id)\n    .log_param_string (\"gmsgid\", gmsgid);\n  auto_inc_log_depth depth_sentinel (logger);\n\n  auto_diagnostic_group d;\n  va_list ap;\n  va_start (ap, gmsgid);\n  bool ret = (\"emit_diagnostic_valist_meta\", ret);\n\n  return ret;\n}\n\n/* An informative note at LOCATION.
